A graduate of Howard University in DC, Mrs. Haynes paved the way for individuals like my self to aspire to be successful journalist as well as strong and courageous woman. Comment: aaronricketts_ said "I am choosing this image for my entry in the @nikonusa #IAmNextContest because I feel as though it is a great representation of how much I've grown with my photography. I was introduced to the medium back when I was in high school and I've been very passionate about it ever since. What makes me so passionate about it is that it allows me to create images that are not only visually pleasing to the eye but are tools to help me express my feelings on a day to day basis, which is why my favorite style of photography has become a mixture of portraiture and surrealism. Photography has not only allowed me to express my creativity, it has also helped me become more sociable with the world around me, without it I don't think I would be who I am today. With the help of @nikonusa and the images I create with their cameras & lenses I want to continue with the "Art Is" event series I started to not only showcase my work but the work of other artist as well because from my experience it can be somewhat difficult to have your work/message seen or heard and I believe our Generation has a lot to offer.

Through our history of working with teen girls, we noticed that, although many had excelled academically in high school, they had not been receiving the skills necessary for their progression into young adulthood and college. We wanted to create a platform that would meet this deficit for not just our programs' students and mentees, but for all qualifying teen girls in Philadelphia.It is our goal to help young ladies between the ages of 13-18 (must be in high school) to reach successful milestones by exploring the possibilities of their future (dreams) and mapping out their individual success plans.
